              <h1 class="field field--name-field-tabloid-headline field--type-string field--label-hidden field__item content-title teaser_lede">
               <a href="/news/matt-jones-routs-field-wins-first-tour-event-seven-years-honda-classic" hreflang="en">
                Jones routs Honda field for first title in 7 years
               </a>
              </h1>
              <div class="byline byline--horizontal">
               <span class="author byline__name">
                BY
                <a href="/author/associated-press" hreflang="en">
                 Associated Press
                </a>
               </span>
               <span class="byline__date">
                —
                <time class="datetime" datetime="2021-03-21T22:34:01Z">
                 March 21, 2021 at  6:34 PM
                </time>
               </span>
              </div>
              <p>
               Matt Jones won his first PGA Tour event in seven years, tying a record margin of victory in The Honda Classic.
              </p>
              <span class="rdf-meta hidden" content="Matt Jones routs field, wins first Tour event in seven years at Honda Classic" property="schema:name">
              </span>
             </div>

                 </time>

                 </a>
                </h1>
                <div class="byline">
                 <span class="author byline__name">
                  BY
                  <a href="/author/golf-channel-digital" hreflang="en">
                   Golf Channel Digital
                  </a>

                 <p class="body__text">
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  Matt Jones captured The Honda Classic, but he wasn't the only big winner on Sunday. So, too, was runner-up Brandon Hagy.
                 </p>
                </div>

                <h1 class="headline">
                 <a href="/news/one-back-nine-play-aaron-wise-four-putts-triple-bogey-honda-classic" hreflang="en">
                  One back at Honda, Wise 4-putts for triple
                 </a>
                </h1>
                <div class="byline">
                 <span class="author byline__name">
                  BY
                  <a href="/author/golf-channel-digital" hreflang="en">
                   Golf Channel Digital
                  </a>
                 </span>
                 <span class="byline__date">
                  —
                  <time class="datetime" datetime="2021-03-21T22:10:00Z">
                   March 21, 2021
                  </time>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="body">
                 <p class="body__text">
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  Aaron Wise was one shot back with nine holes to play at the Honda Classic before four-putting the par-4 10th.
                 </p>
                </div>

              <h1 class="field field--name-field-tabloid-headline field--type-string field--label-hidden field__item content-title teaser_lede">
               <a href="/video/matt-jones-snaps-winless-drought-pga-tour-honda-classic" hreflang="en">
                Jones snaps drought on PGA Tour at The Honda Classic
               </a>
              </h1>
              <div class="video-lede__text">
               Matt Jones (68) says it was worth the wait after seven years between PGA Tour wins following his victory at The Honda Classic
              </div>
             </div>
            </section>

                <a href="/author/amy-rogers" hreflang="en">
                 Amy Rogers
                </a>
               </span>
               <span class="byline__date">
                —
                <time class="datetime" datetime="2021-03-17T12:15:00Z">
                 March 17, 2021 at  8:15 AM
                </time>
               </span>
              </div>
              <p>
               A look back through the decades at some of the most pioneering women in the history of the LPGA Tour.
              </p>
              <span class="rdf-meta hidden" content="LPGA trailblazers: From the founders to the new generation" property="schema:name">
              </span>
             </div>
            </section>
            <div class="paragraph paragraph--type--homepage-section-list-horizontal paragraph--view-mode--default">
             <div about="/node/1413291" class="node node--type-external-links node--view-mode-teaser-horizontal teaser teaser--horizontal mb-6" role="article">
              <div class="row">
               <div class="col lg:col-8">
                <a class="block" href="https://www.lpga.com/news/2021/the-womens-game-greatest-forgotten-champion-stirling" target="_blank">
                 <div class="photo">
                  <img alt="Alexa Stirling" class="image-style-content-section-thumbnail" height="180" src="/sites/default/files/styles/content_section_thumbnail/public/2021/03/18/stirling_1920_historic.jpg?itok=j9zab44I" typeof="foaf:Image" width="320"/>
                 </div>
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="col lg:col-16">
                <a href="https://www.lpga.com/news/2021/the-womens-game-greatest-forgotten-champion-stirling" target="_blank">
                 <span class="field field--name-field-content-label field--type-string field--label-above tag">
                  <span>
                   LPGA
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </a>
                <a href="https://www.lpga.com/news/2021/the-womens-game-greatest-forgotten-champion-stirling" target="_blank">
                 <h1 class="headline">
                  Alexa Stirling: Women's golf's greatest forgotten champion
                 </h1>
                </a>
                <div class="body pt-3">
                 <p>
                  She's often remembered for her connection to Bobby Jones, but Alexa Stirling was the greatest female player in the world during the WWI era.
                 </p>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </section>
           <section class="paragraph paragraph--type--homepage-section paragraph--view-mode--default homepage-section homepage-section-separator">
